How to work a req: check internal TalentBase coverage first (every count opens to real candidate records in the app), then run Net 1 → Net 2 → Net 3 in LinkedIn Recruiter using the copy buttons, then send the InMail sequence (initial → day 3-4 → day 7-8 → day 12-14 close). Every message asks for interest, a current resume, and availability. Limited-confidence = no JD on file (105 of 129) — confirm scope with the HM before spending InMail credits. Merge fields {FIRST} and {COMPANY} personalize per candidate.

Algorithms / AI Engineering (Merrimack NH)

1 requisition · 1490
▶
Principal algorithm and AI engineering for defense sensing and autonomy — where models meet fielded hardware.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect 30-100 profiles
Title
("Algorithm Engineer" OR "AI Engineer" OR "Machine Learning Engineer" OR "Research Scientist" OR "Perception Engineer") AND (Principal OR Staff OR Senior OR Lead)
Keywords
(algorithm OR "machine learning" OR "computer vision" OR perception OR "sensor fusion" OR tracking OR "signal processing") AND (C++ OR Python OR MATLAB) AND (defense OR aerospace OR radar OR EO/IR OR autonomy)
Filters: Location: New England + national (pool is national). Years: 10+. Industry: Defense & Space, Research.
Run notes: Elite pool — every profile is a named target.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 200-500 profiles
Title
("Machine Learning" OR "Computer Vision" OR "Algorithm" OR "Perception" OR "Autonomy")
Keywords
(deep learning OR CNN OR tracking OR estimation OR Kalman OR "signal processing" OR embedded ML) AND (deploy OR production OR "real-time" OR edge)
Filters: Location: United States. Years: 7+. Target defense-AI companies + labs.
Run notes: Raid net — defense-AI startups + FFRDC staff.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 800+ profiles
Title
("Machine Learning Engineer" OR "AI" OR "Data Scientist" OR "Research Engineer")
Keywords
("computer vision" OR perception OR "sensor" OR "signal processing") AND (PhD OR MS OR research)
Filters: Location: United States + top-program alumni (MIT, CMU, Stanford, Georgia Tech). Years: 5+.
Run notes: Discovery net; screen for real-time/edge deployment (not notebook-only).

Target Companies

Tier 1 — direct competitors: MIT Lincoln LaboratoryDraperSTR (Woburn MA)Charles River Analytics (Cambridge)RTX BBN (Cambridge)AndurilShield AI
Tier 2 — adjacent industry: Palantir (defense)Scale AI (federal)Raytheon / Lockheed AI orgsMITREKitwareAretéSystems & Technology Research
Tier 3 — feeders & converts: autonomy startups (Skydio, Zipline alumni)MIT/CMU robotics lab alumniquant researchers seeking mission (occasionally convert)

Exclusions

Exclude notebook-only data scientists without deployment record; exclude non-US-persons (ITAR); exclude current Elbit employees; exclude candidates already on req 1490.

InMail Sequence (family template — per-req personalized versions inside each req below)

Subjects: Algorithms that fly, not just fit | Principal Algorithm/AI — {LOC} | Edge AI with consequences
Initial InMail
{FIRST} — your work in perception/algorithms stood out. I am recruiting a {ROLE} in {LOC} for Elbit Systems of America: principal-level algorithm and AI development for defense sensing — tracking, fusion, real-time inference on fielded hardware, where 'production' means an aircraft, not a dashboard. It is the rare seat combining research-grade problems with deployment discipline, on funded programs. Southern NH, no state income tax, Boston research community in reach. If a 15-minute conversation is warranted, reply with a current resume and two windows this week. — Jonah Adelman, The Staffing Specialist (retained recruiting partner to Elbit America)
Follow-up 1 · day 3-4
{FIRST} — resurfacing. The {ROLE} seat is one-of-one and the shortlist is short by nature of the field. Resume + two time windows and I will bring the technical specifics.
Follow-up 2 · day 7-8
{FIRST} — the honest differentiator: your models ship on hardware with SWaP limits and lives attached — the constraints that make the work interesting. If notebook-to-nowhere is wearing on you, this is the antidote. 15 minutes?
Follow-up 3 · day 12-14 (close)
{FIRST} — final note. If the timing is off, a resume on file keeps you first for the next senior algorithms seat. This community is small — a referral to a peer is gold and repaid. Thanks either way.
Verify on first call: Verify deployment record (what hardware, what latency), US-person status, and depth vs breadth (principal seat needs depth).
Flexibility: HM open to radar/RF signal-processing depth in lieu of EO/IR; C++ deployment fluency is the constant.

Cybersecurity — Engineering, GRC, Cloud, Vulnerability Management (Fort Worth TX · Remote-eligible)

5 requisitions · 1277, 1241, 1268, 1284, 1324
▶
Defending defense — enterprise and product security for a US defense manufacturer: RMF, cloud, vulnerability management and compliance at mission scale.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect 50-150 profiles (national: 400+)
Title
("Cyber Security Engineer" OR "Cybersecurity Engineer" OR "Security Engineer" OR "Cloud Engineer" OR "GRC" OR "Vulnerability Management") AND (Senior OR Principal OR Manager OR Lead)
Keywords
(RMF OR "NIST 800-171" OR "NIST 800-53" OR CMMC OR eMASS OR ATO OR ISSM OR ISSO OR "vulnerability management" OR Tenable OR Qualys OR CrowdStrike) AND (defense OR DoD OR cleared OR CUI)
Filters: Location: DFW 40 mi; req 1277 remote-eligible — run national in parallel. Years: 5+ (Senior Mgr: 10+). Industry: Defense, IT Services, Computer & Network Security.
Run notes: Cleared-cyber pool; certifications (CISSP, Security+) are strong markers.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 300-800 profiles
Title
("Security Engineer" OR "Information Security" OR "Cloud Security" OR "DevSecOps" OR "Security Analyst" OR "Compliance Manager")
Keywords
(CISSP OR CISM OR "Security+" OR CEH OR AWS OR Azure) AND (security OR compliance OR vulnerability OR incident) AND (enterprise OR federal OR regulated)
Filters: Location: Texas + national for remote req. Years: 4+. Target federal integrators + finance/healthcare security orgs.
Run notes: Core net; finance/healthcare security staff convert to defense with citizenship.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 1,500+ profiles
Title
("Security" AND (Engineer OR Analyst OR Manager OR Architect))
Keywords
(cybersecurity OR "information security" OR infosec) AND (cloud OR network OR endpoint OR GRC)
Filters: Location: United States. Years: 3+. Filter: US citizenship signals (clearance, federal, military).
Run notes: Discovery net; screen hard for US-person + hands-on depth.

Target Companies

Tier 1 — direct competitors: Lockheed Martin (Fort Worth)Raytheon / RTXL3HarrisBooz Allen HamiltonLeidosSAICPeratonCACIManTech
Tier 2 — adjacent industry: BellGeneral Dynamics ITNorthrop GrummanDeloitte GPS cyberAccenture FederalMITREAir Force / Army cyber veterans (17C, 1B4)
Tier 3 — feeders & converts: USAA (San Antonio)Bank of America / Schwab / Fidelity security (DFW)American Airlines cybersecurityCrowdStrike / Rapid7 / Tenable field engineersMSSPs

Exclusions

Exclude non-US-person profiles (clearance path required); exclude pure physical-security profiles; exclude current Elbit employees; exclude candidates already assigned in TalentBase.

InMail Sequence (family template — per-req personalized versions inside each req below)

Initial InMail

This is consequential security: CUI and cleared environments, RMF/CMMC reality, modern tooling, and adversaries that are not hypothetical. Funded, stable, and the mission writes itself. If you hold or can hold a clearance, you are ahead of the line. 15 minutes to compare notes? Reply with a current resume and two windows this week. — Jonah Adelman, The Staffing Specialist (retained recruiting partner to Elbit America)
Follow-up 1 · day 3-4
{FIRST} — bumping this. The {ROLE} role is active and cleared-eligible profiles like yours are the constraint, not the req. Resume + two time windows and I will get you specifics fast.
Follow-up 2 · day 7-8
{FIRST} — one more angle: defense security careers compound — clearance, CMMC scars and RMF fluency only get more valuable. This seat builds all three while paying competitively today. Worth a look? Send availability and a resume.
Follow-up 3 · day 12-14 (close)
{FIRST} — closing out. If the timing is off, a resume on file means first-call on the next security seat (this org is growing its cyber bench). A referral to a sharp cleared engineer is always repaid. Thanks either way.
Verify on first call: Verify US citizenship/clearance eligibility first; hands-on vs paper-compliance balance per req; for Cloud Engineer verify IaC depth.
Flexibility: Req 1277 is remote-eligible — use it to win candidates the DFW reqs cannot; finance/healthcare security converts with citizenship.

▶
Electrical design for electro-optics and defense products — board and system level, II through Staff, at sites where EEs own hardware end-to-end.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect 20-80 profiles local; national widens
Title
("Electrical Engineer" OR "Hardware Engineer" OR "Electronics Engineer") AND (II OR Senior OR Staff OR Principal)
Keywords
("circuit design" OR schematic OR PCB OR analog OR digital OR FPGA OR "power supply") AND (Altium OR OrCAD OR Cadence) AND (defense OR aerospace OR electro-optic OR sensor OR military)
Filters: Location: per req anchor (Roanoke 30 mi; site-code reqs: national until site confirmed). Years: per level (II: 2-5, Senior: 5+, Staff/Principal: 10+). Industry: Defense & Space, Electronics.
Run notes: Roanoke EE pool is thin — expect to run Nets 2-3 early.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 150-450 profiles
Title
("Electrical Engineer" OR "Hardware Design Engineer" OR "Design Engineer")
Keywords
(schematic OR PCB OR "circuit design" OR embedded hardware OR FPGA OR VHDL OR mixed-signal) AND (product OR hardware) AND (test OR qualification OR EMC)
Filters: Location: VA/NC/TN corridor (Blacksburg, Lynchburg, Charlottesville, Raleigh, Knoxville) + relocation-open. Years: per level. Veteran filter on.
Run notes: Core net; VT ECE alumni are the regional feeder.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 1,000+ profiles
Title
("Electrical Engineer" OR "Hardware Engineer")
Keywords
("circuit design" OR PCB OR analog OR power electronics) AND (defense OR aerospace OR industrial OR automotive)
Filters: Location: United States, Open to Work + relocation. Years: per level.
Run notes: Relocation net — Blue Ridge cost-of-living pitch works on mid-career EEs.

Target Companies

▶
Growth leadership for a defense manufacturer — capture, customer intimacy and next-generation concepts from maritime to launched effects.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect 40-150 profiles
Title
("Business Development" AND (VP OR "Vice President" OR Director OR "Senior Director")) OR "Capture Manager" OR "Growth Officer"
Keywords
(capture OR "business development" OR pipeline OR "customer engagement" OR proposal) AND (defense OR DoD OR Navy OR maritime OR Army OR unmanned OR "launched effects") AND (prime OR program)
Filters: Location: national (executive search — relocation assumed). Years: 15+. Industry: Defense & Space.
Run notes: Executive pool; treat as named-target search with referral mapping.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 100-300 profiles
Title
("Business Development" OR Capture OR "Strategy Director" OR "Program Director")
Keywords
(shipbuilding OR maritime OR USV OR UUV OR "unmanned systems" OR "advanced concepts" OR DARPA OR "rapid capabilities") AND (capture OR growth OR customer)
Filters: Location: national + DC-metro emphasis (customer proximity). Years: 12+. Maritime req: Navy/shipbuilder networks. Advanced-concepts req: DARPA/RCO ecosystem.
Run notes: Domain nets per seat — maritime and advanced-concepts pools barely overlap.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 400+ profiles
Title
(Director OR VP) AND (Defense OR Aerospace OR Government)
Keywords
(strategy OR growth OR capture OR "customer relationships") AND (military OR federal)
Filters: Location: national. Years: 12+. Include transitioning senior military officers (O-5/O-6) with acquisition or operational credibility.
Run notes: Discovery net; senior-officer transitions are strong for maritime/advanced-concepts seats.

Target Companies

Tier 1 — direct competitors: HII (Huntington Ingalls)Austal USAFincantieri MarinetteAnduril (maritime + advanced)SaronicTextron SystemsL3Harris maritimeLeidos (Gibbs & Cox)
Tier 2 — adjacent industry: Lockheed / Raytheon / NG BD execsGeneral Dynamics Mission SystemsKratosAeroVironmentShield AIBoeing Phantom Works alumniDARPA / ONR / NavSea civilian leaders
Tier 3 — feeders & converts: transitioning O-5/O-6 (SWO, aviation, acquisition corps)boutique defense-strategy consultancies (Avascent, Renaissance)venture-backed defense-tech CROs

Filters: Location: per req anchor (Roanoke 30 mi / DFW 40 mi / Merrimack 30 mi). Years: per level (I: 0-3, II: 2-5, III/Sr: 5+). Industry: Defense & Space, Accounting.
Run notes: GovCon-finance precision pool; DFW is deep (Lockheed FW finance org).
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 250-700 per site

6 requisitions · 663, 810, 845, 1265, 1500, 1572
▶
Defense program management — cost, schedule and performance on funded DoD programs, from sustainment through new starts.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect 50-180 profiles
Title
("Program Manager" OR "Program Scheduler" OR "Master Scheduler") AND (II OR III OR Senior OR Master)
Keywords
(EVMS OR "earned value" OR "integrated master schedule" OR IMS OR "cost account" OR CDRL OR "DoD program" OR sustainment) AND (defense OR aerospace OR government)
Filters: Location: per req anchor (DFW 40 mi / Merrimack 30 mi). Years: PM II 5+, PM III 8+. Industry: Defense & Space, Aviation & Aerospace.
Run notes: DFW is the deepest defense-PM market in the country outside DC.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 250-600 profiles
Title
("Program Manager" OR "Project Manager" OR "IPT Lead" OR "Program Management")
Keywords
(PMP OR EVMS OR milestone OR "cost schedule" OR risk OR stakeholder) AND (defense OR aerospace OR manufacturing OR engineering)
Filters: Location: widen 60 mi + relocation-open for PM III. Years: 5+. Include transitioning military acquisition officers (keywords: DAWIA, acquisition corps).
Run notes: Core net — military acquisition officers are an elite feeder.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 1,000+ profiles
Title
("Program Manager" OR "Project Manager")
Keywords
(program OR project) AND (hardware OR engineering OR manufacturing OR government)
Filters: Location: metro per site. Years: 4+.
Run notes: Discovery net; screen hard for hardware-program scope vs IT-project scope.

Target Companies

Tier 1 — direct competitors: Lockheed Martin (Fort Worth — F-35 program office alumni)BellRaytheon (McKinney)L3Harris (Greenville)General DynamicsBAE Systems (Nashua NH)Northrop Grumman
Tier 2 — adjacent industry: Textron SystemsCollins AerospaceLeonardo DRSKratosAmentum / KBR / V2X (sustainment PMs)Draper / MITRE program staff
Tier 3 — feeders & converts: military acquisition officers (DAWIA II/III) transitioningPMI chapter leadership (PMP+defense)aerospace suppliers' program offices (Triumph, Spirit)

Exclusions

Exclude IT/software-only project managers; exclude current Elbit employees; exclude candidates already assigned in TalentBase.

Systems Engineering — GNC / Environmental Qualification (Merrimack NH)

2 requisitions · 1381, 925
▶
Guidance, navigation and control plus environmental-qualification systems work on fielded defense programs that protect aircrews and warfighters.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect 25-80 profiles
Title
("Systems Engineer" OR "GNC Engineer" OR "Guidance Navigation and Control" OR "Flight Controls Engineer") AND (Senior OR Staff OR Principal OR Lead)
Keywords
(GNC OR "guidance navigation" OR autopilot OR "flight control") AND (Kalman OR "six degree" OR 6DOF OR "state estimation" OR simulation) AND (MATLAB OR Simulink) AND (defense OR aerospace OR missile OR munition)
Filters: Location: Merrimack NH 25 mi. Years: 8+. Industry: Defense & Space, Aviation & Aerospace. Keywords add: clearance OR secret.
Run notes: Small, high-precision pool. Review every profile.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 150-450 profiles
Title
("Systems Engineer" OR "Guidance Engineer" OR "Controls Engineer" OR "Aerospace Engineer" OR "Flight Dynamics")
Keywords
(GNC OR guidance OR autopilot OR "flight dynamics" OR "environmental qualification" OR "MIL-STD-810" OR qualification) AND (aerospace OR defense) AND (requirements OR integration OR verification)
Filters: Location: Greater Boston + southern NH 50 mi (Tewksbury, Andover, Burlington, Cambridge, Nashua). Years: 5+. Industry: Defense & Space, Aviation & Aerospace, Research.
Run notes: Core working net — commute-tested Boston-north defense corridor.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 600-2,000 profiles
Title
("Systems Engineer" OR "GNC" OR "Guidance" OR "Flight Controls" OR "Aerospace Engineer")
Keywords
(GNC OR guidance OR Kalman OR autopilot OR "flight control" OR "MIL-STD-810") AND (missile OR munition OR UAS OR aircraft OR spacecraft)
Filters: Location: United States, filter Open to Work + open to relocation. Years: 5+.
Run notes: Relocation net. NH has no state income tax — use as the relocation hook.

Target Companies

Tier 1 — direct competitors: Raytheon / RTX (Tewksbury, Andover MA)BAE Systems (Nashua NH, Merrimack NH)Draper (Cambridge MA)MIT Lincoln Laboratory (Lexington MA)Textron Systems (Wilmington MA)General Dynamics Mission SystemsL3Harris

Tier 3 — feeders & converts: Shield AISkydioBoston-area aero/robotics startupsMIT / Draper fellows and lab alumniBoeing (former NE staff)

Exclusions

Exclude current Elbit Systems of America employees; candidates already active on this req in TalentBase; interns/new grads (Net 1-2).

Systems Engineering — Integration / V&V (Roanoke VA · Fort Worth TX · Merrimack NH)

12 requisitions · 1263, 1329, 1448, 1356, 1357, 1411, 1481, 1504, 1538, 1539, 1540, 1560
▶
Systems engineering across electro-optics, force protection and fielded defense products — requirements through integration, verification and field support.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect 30-120 profiles (Roanoke low end, DFW high end)
Title
("Systems Engineer" OR "Systems Integration Engineer") AND (Senior OR Staff OR Principal OR II)
Keywords
("systems engineering" OR integration OR "V&V" OR verification) AND (requirements OR DOORS OR MBSE OR SysML) AND (defense OR aerospace OR "electro-optic" OR EO/IR OR sensor)
Filters: Location: per req anchor (Roanoke 30 mi / DFW 35 mi / Merrimack 25 mi). Years: 5+. Industry: Defense & Space.
Run notes: Precision pool; review all.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 200-600 profiles
Title
("Systems Engineer" OR "Integration Engineer" OR "Test and Integration" OR "Requirements Engineer" OR "Field Service Engineer")
Keywords
(requirements OR integration OR verification OR DOORS OR MBSE OR "system of systems") AND (defense OR aerospace OR military OR radar OR EW OR "night vision" OR sensor)
Filters: Location: widen — VA statewide + Greensboro/Raleigh NC for ROA; TX statewide for FWO; Boston metro for MER. Years: 3+. Add veteran filter: military background.
Run notes: Core working net; prioritize cleared and veteran profiles.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 1,000-3,000 profiles
Title
("Systems Engineer" OR "Integration Engineer" OR "Project Engineer")
Keywords
(requirements OR integration OR verification OR validation) AND (defense OR aerospace OR DoD)
Filters: Location: United States, open-to-relocation + Open to Work. Years: 3+.
Run notes: Relocation net — sell low cost of living (ROA), no state tax (TX/NH).

Target Companies

Tier 1 — direct competitors: Northrop Grumman (Charlottesville VA)L3HarrisBAE Systems (Radford VA ordnance; Nashua NH)Lockheed MartinRaytheon / RTXGeneral DynamicsCollins AerospaceLeonardo DRS
Tier 2 — adjacent industry: BWX Technologies (Lynchburg VA)Framatome (Lynchburg VA)LeidosSAICBooz Allen HamiltonAmentumKBRBell (Fort Worth)
Tier 3 — feeders & converts: Virginia Tech Hume Center alumniTorc Robotics (Blacksburg)military veterans (94/25/35-series, Navy ET/FC, USAF 2A)Micron (Manassas VA)

Exclusions

Exclude current Elbit Systems of America employees; candidates already assigned to this req in TalentBase; pure-IT 'systems engineers' (sysadmin profiles) — the keyword net filters most, screen the rest.

Test Engineering (Roanoke VA · Fort Worth TX)

3 requisitions · 1267, 1321, 1555
▶
Test engineering for electro-optics and guided-munitions programs — ATE, environmental test and production test on hardware that must not fail in the field.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect 30-120 profiles
Title
("Test Engineer" OR "Test Engineering") AND (Senior OR Principal OR Lead)
Keywords
(ATE OR "automated test" OR LabVIEW OR TestStand OR "environmental test" OR "MIL-STD-810" OR qualification) AND (defense OR aerospace OR munition OR missile OR electro-optic)
Filters: Location: per req (Roanoke 30 mi / DFW 35 mi). Years: 5+ (Principal: 10+). Industry: Defense & Space, Aviation & Aerospace.
Run notes: Precision pool; DFW is deep for munitions test.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 200-500 profiles
Title
("Test Engineer" OR "Validation Engineer" OR "Hardware Test" OR "Integration and Test")
Keywords
(LabVIEW OR TestStand OR Python OR "test fixture" OR "test procedure" OR ESS OR HASS OR vibration OR thermal) AND (electronics OR hardware OR avionics)
Filters: Location: widen per anchor (VA statewide / TX). Years: 3+. Veteran filter on — military test/avionics backgrounds convert well.
Run notes: Core working net.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 800-2,000 profiles
Title
("Test Engineer" OR "Test Technician" OR "Quality Engineer")
Keywords
(test OR ATE OR LabVIEW OR qualification) AND (defense OR aerospace OR automotive OR electronics)
Filters: Location: United States, relocation-open. Years: 3+.
Run notes: Discovery net; adjacent-industry test engineers (auto, rail, semicon) convert.

Target Companies

Tier 1 — direct competitors: Lockheed Martin (Fort Worth / Grand Prairie)Raytheon (McKinney/Tucson munitions)L3HarrisGeneral Dynamics OTSNorthrop GrummanBAE Systems (Radford VA)Textron Systems

Tier 3 — feeders & converts: NI/Emerson Test & Measurement ecosystem engineersAverna / ATS automation integratorsVolvo Trucks (Dublin VA) testWabtec (Salem VA) testmilitary ATE veterans (Navy AT, USAF 2A6)

Exclusions
